\DoxyCodeLine{00006\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ tuple\_vector\ is\ a\ data\ container\ that\ is\ designed\ to\ abstract\ and\ simplify}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00007\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ the\ handling\ of\ a\ "{}structure\ of\ arrays"{}\ layout\ of\ data\ in\ memory.\ In}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00008\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ particular,\ it\ mimics\ the\ interface\ of\ vector,\ including\ functionality\ to\ do}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00009\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ inserts,\ erases,\ push\_backs,\ and\ random-\/access.\ It\ also\ provides\ a}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00010\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ RandomAccessIterator\ and\ corresponding\ functionality,\ making\ it\ compatible}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00011\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ with\ most\ STL\ (and\ STL-\/esque)\ algorithms\ such\ as\ ranged-\/for\ loops,\ find\_if,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00012\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ remove\_if,\ or\ sort.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00013\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{00014\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ When\ used\ or\ applied\ properly,\ this\ container\ can\ improve\ performance\ of}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00015\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ some\ algorithms\ through\ cache-\/coherent\ data\ accesses\ or\ allowing\ for}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00016\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ sensible\ SIMD\ programming,\ while\ keeping\ the\ structure\ of\ a\ single}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00017\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ container,\ to\ permit\ a\ developer\ to\ continue\ to\ use\ existing\ algorithms\ in}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00018\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ STL\ and\ the\ like.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00019\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00020\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Consult\ doc/Bonus/tuple\_vector\_readme.md\ for\ more\ information.}}
